Mitrao, bachpan mein padhi ye kahani aaj bhi musibat ke kshanon mein dhairya rakhne ki prerna deti hai, taaki hum kathin samay ka dat kar muqabla kar sakein. Doosre, mitrata ka sadaiv samman karein.
Ek nadi ke kinaare, ek jamun ke ped par, ek bandar reh­ta tha, jiski mitrata, us nadi mein rehne wale magarmach ke saath ho gayi. Wo bandar, us magarmach ko bhi khane ke liye jamun deta rehta tha. Ek din, us magarmach ne, kuch jamun, apni patni ko bhi khilaye. Swadisht jamun khane ke baad, usne ye sochkar ki rozana aise meethi phal khane wale ka dil bhi khoob meetha hoga, apne pati se, us bandar ka dil lane ki zidd ki. Patni ke haathon majboor hue magarmach ne bhi ek chaal chali, aur bandar se kaha, ki uski bhabhi, use milna chahti hai. Isliye, wo uski peeth par baith jaye, taaki surakshit us ghar pahunch jaye. Bandar bhi apne mitr ki baat ka bharosa kar, ped se nadi mein kooda, aur uski peeth par, savaar ho gaya. Jab ve nadi ke beecon-beech pahuche, magarmach ne socha, ki ab bandar ko sahi baat batane mein, koi haani nahi, aur usne bhed khol diya ki uski patni, uska dil, khana chahti hai. Bandar ko dhakka toh laga, lekin usne, apna dhairya nahi khoya, aur tapak se bola, Oh, tumne ye baat mujhe pehle kyun nahi batayi, kyunki maine toh apna dil, jamun ke ped ki khokhal mein sambhal kar rakha hai. Ab jaldi se mujhe wapas nadi ke kinaare le chalo, taaki main apna dil laakar, apni bhabhi ko uphaar mein dekar, use khush kar sakun. Moorkh magarmach, bandar ko jaise hi nadi kinaare le kar aaya, bandar ne zor se jamun ke ped par chhalang lagayi, aur krodh mein bharkar bola, Are moorkh, dil ke bina bhi kya koi zinda reh sakta hai? Ja, aaj se teri-meri dosti samaapt.
Mitraon, hamari zindagi mein shabd, bahut maayne rakhte hain. Dono hi din, cheeta to wahi tha, usme wahi furti aur wahi taakat thi. Par jis din, use discourage kiya gaya, wo asafal ho gaya. Jis din, encourage kiya gaya, wo safal ho gaya.
Ek baar, do gadhe, apni peeth par bojha uthaye chale ja rahe the, unko kaafi lamba safar tay karna tha. Ek gadhe ki peeth par, namak ki bhaari boriyan ladi hui thi, to ek ki peeth par, rui ki boriyan ladi hui thi.
Agli subah, wo ek baar phir shikaar ke liye nikla. Kuch door jaane par, use ek boodhe bandar ne dekha aur poocha, kahaan ja rahe ho beta? Bandar mama, main shikaar par ja raha hoon, cheetah bola. Bahut achhe, bandar bola. Tumhari taakat aur gati ke kaaran, tum ek behad kushal shikari ban sakte ho. Jao, tumhe jald hi safalta milegi. Ye sun, cheetah utsah se bhar gaya, aur kuch hi samay mein, usne, chote se hiran ka shikaar kar liya.
Ek sant, ye saara kissa, apne shishyon ke saath dekh rahe the. Unhone apne shishyon se kaha, manushya ko sada apna vivek jagrit rakhna chahiye. Bina apni buddhi lagaye, doosron ki nakal kar vaisa hi karne wale sada upahash ke patra bante hain.
Ek naujawan cheetah, pehli baar shikar karne nikla. Abhi wo kuch hi aage badha tha, ki ek lakadbaggha, use rokate hue bola, Are chotu, kahan ja rahe ho tum? Main to aaj pehli baar khud se shikar karne nikla hoon!, cheetah romanchit hote hue bola. Lakadbaggha hansa, abhi to tumhare khelne-koodne ke din hain, tum itne chhote ho, tumhe shikar karne ka koi anubhav bhi nahi hai. Tum kya shikar karoge! Lakadbagghay ki baat sunkar, cheetah udaas ho gaya. Din bhar shikar ke liye wo beman idhar-udhar ghoomta raha, kuch ek prayaas bhi kiye, par safalta nahi mili, aur use bhookhe pet hi ghar lautna pada.
Mitron, hamari asal zindagi mein bhi ye baat laagu hoti hai. Hum kisi ko ek kshetra mein safal hote dekh, use copy karna shuru kar dete hain. Hume lagta hai, ki yadi koi banda apne kshetra mein safal ho gaya, to hume bhi us kshetra mein safalta mil jaayegi. Lekin hum shayad ye dhyaan nahi dete, ki uski peeth par, namak wali kaari hai, matlab, uska interest alag hai, aur bhoolvash, hum rui ki kaari ko laade, chhalang laga dete hain, matlab, doosre talent ya interest ko laade us kshetra mein safal hone ka khwab dekhte hai, aur antatah hume pachhtana padta hai. Isliye, doosron ko dekhkar seekhna theek hai, par unka andha anukaran karna, us moorkh gadhe ke samaan vyavhaar karna hai.
Jis raaste se wo ja rahe the, us beech mein ek nadi padi. Nadi ke upar ret ki boriyon ka kaccha pul bana hua tha. Jis gadhe ki peeth par namak ki boriyan thi, uska pair, buri tarah se fisal gaya, aur wo nadi ke andar gir pada. Nadi mein girte hi, namak paani mein ghul gaya, aur uska vazan, halka ho gaya. Wo ye baat, badi prasannata se dusre ko batane laga. Dusre gadhe ne socha, ye to badhiya yukti hai, aise mein to main bhi apna bhaar, kaafi kam kar sakta hoon, aur usne bina soche samjhe, paani mein chhalang laga di. Kintu rui ke paani sokh lene ke kaaran, uska bhaar kam hone ki jagah, bahut badh gaya, jis kaaran, wo murkh gadha, paani mein doob gaya.
Bahut samay pehle ki baat hai, sudoor dakshin mein, kisi pratapi raja ka rajya tha. Raja ke teen putra the. Ek din, raja ke man mein aaya, ki putron ko, kuch aisi shiksha di jaye, ki samay aane par wo raj-kaaj sambhal saken. Isi vichar ke saath, raja ne sabhi putron ko darbar mein bulaya aur bola, putron, hamare rajya mein, nashpati ka koi vriksh nahi hai. Main chahta hoon tum sab chaar-chaar mahine ke antaraal par is vriksh ki talash mein jao, aur pata lagao ki wo kaisa hota hai? Raja ki aagya paa kar teenon putra, baari-baari se gaye, aur wapas laut aaye.
Sabhi putron ke laut aane par, raja ne punah, sabhi ko darbar mein bulaya, aur us ped ke baare mein batane ko kaha. Pehla putra bola, Pitaji, wo ped to bilkul tedha-meadha aur sukha hua tha. Nahin-nahin, wo to bilkul hara-bhara tha, lekin shayad usme kuch kami thi, kyunki uspar, ek bhi phal, nahin laga tha, dusre putra ne pehle ko beech mein hi rokate hue kaha. Phir teesra putra bola, Bhaiya, lagta hai, aap bhi koi galat ped dekh aaye, kyunki maine sachmuch nashpati ka ped dekha. Wo bahut hi shandaar tha, aur phalon se lada pada tha. Aur teeno putra, apni-apni baat ko lekar aapas mein vivaad karne lage, ki tabhi raja, apne singhasan se uthe, aur bole, putron, tumhe aapas mein behas karne ki koi avashyakta nahin hai. Darasal tum teeno hi vriksh ka sahi varnana kar rahe ho. Maine jaanboojh kar, tumhe alag-alag mausam mein, vriksh khojne bheja tha, aur tumne jo dekha, wo us mausam ke anusaar tha.
Main chahta hoon, ki is anubhav ke aadhar par, tum teen baaton ko gaanth baandh lo. Pehli, kisi cheez ke baare mein sahi aur poorn jankari chahiye, to tumhe use lambe samay tak dekhna-parakhna chahiye. Phir chahe wo koi vishay ho, vastu ho, ya phir, koi vyakti hi kyon na ho. Dusri, har mausam ek sa nahi hota. Jis prakar vriksh mausam ke anusaar sookhta, hara-bhara, ya phalon se lada rehta hai, usi prakar, manushya ke jeevan mein bhi, utaar chadhaav aate rehte hain. Atah, agar tum kabhi bhi bure daur se guzar rahe ho, to apni himmat aur dhairya, banaye rakho. Samay avashya badalta hai. Aur teesri baat, apni baat ko hi sahi maan kar us par ade mat raho. Apna dimaag kholo, aur doosron ke vichaaron ko bhi jaano. Ye sansaar gyaan se bhara pada hai. Chah kar bhi, tum akele saara gyaan arjit nahi kar sakte. Isliye, bhram ki sthiti mein, kisi gyani vyakti se salah lene mein sankoch mat karo.
Bahut samay pehle ki baat hai, Himalay ke jungleon mein, ek bahut taakatwar sher rehta tha. Ek din, usne baarasinghe ka shikar kiya, aur khane ke baad, apni gufa ko lautne laga. Abhi usne chalna shuru hi kiya tha, ki ek siyār, uske saamne dandavat karta hua, uske gunagaan karne laga. Use dekh sher ne poocha, are! tum ye kya kar rahe ho?
Vyavaharik buddhi se, hamara aashay hai, ki kis samay humein kya karna chahiye, aur jo ham kar rahe hain, us karya ka parinaam nikalne par, kya samasyaayein aa sakti hain. Ye sochna hi vyavaharik buddhi hai. Bolchaal ki bhaasha mein ham ise common sense bhi kehte hain, aur bhale hi, ham bade gyaani na hon, moti-moti kitaaben na padhi hon, lekin ham apni vyavaharik buddhi se, kisi paristhiti ka saamna, aasani se kar sakte hain.
Madhyambuddhi aur atibuddhi, apne parampra aur shastra gyaan ko lekar, wahiin ruk gayin. Agle din machhuaron ne poori taiyaari ke saath aakar, vahaan jaal daala, aur un dono ki, ek na chali. Jab machhuare unke vishal shareer ko taang rahe the, tab vyavharikbuddhi ne gheri saans lekar kaha, inke shastra gyaan ne hi dhokha diya. Kaash, inmein thodi, vyavharik buddhi bhi hoti.
Ek din kuch machhuaare, sarovar ke tat par aaye, aur machhliyon ki bahutayat dekhkar, baatein karne lage, ki yahaan kaafi machhliyaan hain, subah aakar, hum ismein jaal daalenge. Unki baatein machhliyon ne suni. Vyavharik buddhi ne kaha, humein fauran ye talaab chhod dena chahiye. Patle soton ka maarg pakadkar, udhar jangli ghaas se dhake hue jangli sarovar mein chale jaana chahiye. Madhyambuddhi ne kaha, pracheen kaal se hamare poorvaj, thand ke dinon mein hi wahan jaate hain, aur abhi to, wo mausam hi nahin aaya hai. Hum hamare varshon se chali aa rahi is parampara ko nahi tod sakte. Machhuaaron ka khatra ho, ya na ho, humein is parampara ka dhyan rakhna hai.
Vyapaari ki baat sunte hi Guru ji saari baat samajh gaye, aur bole, hairani aur pareshani chhodo. Darsal, jo gaon wale pujari hain, unka achha swabhav hi hai, jo log usi devalay mein jaana chahte hain, jahan ve hote hain. Unka logon se nishwarth prem, unke dukh se dukhi hona, unke sukh mein prasann hona, unse mitrata ka vyavhaar karna hi, logon ko, unki aur aakarshit karta hai, aur log svatah hi, unki aur khinche chale aate hain. Ab saari baat, vyapaari ki samajh mein aa chuki thi.
Ek sarovar mein teen divya machhliyan rahti thiin. Wahan ki tamaam machhliyan, un teenon ke prati hi shraddha mein banti hui thiin. Ek machhli ka naam vyavharikbuddhi tha, doosri ka naam madhyambuddhi, aur teesri ka naam, atibuddhi tha. Atibuddhi ke paas, gyaan ka aseem bhandaar tha. Wo sabhi prakaar ke shastroin ka gyaan rakhti thi. Madhyambuddhi ko utni hi dur tak sochne ki aadat thi, jisse uska vaasta padta tha. Wo sochti kam thi, paramparagat dhang se apna kaam kiya karti thi. Vyavharik buddhi, na parampara par dhyaan deti thi, aur na hi shastr par. Use jab jaisi aavashyakta hoti thi, nirnay liya karti thi, aur aavashyakta na padne par kisi shastr ke panne tak nahin ulatati thi.
Atibuddhi ne, garv se hansate hue kaha, tum log ajnani ho, tumhe shastron ka gyaan nahin hai. Jo baadal garazte hain, ve barsate nahin hain. Phir hum log ek hazaar tarikon se tairna jaante hain, paani ke tal mein jaakar baithne ki samarthyata hai. Hamare poonch mein itni shakti hai, ki hum jaalon ko faad sakti hain. Waise bhi kaha gaya hai, ki sankaton se ghire hue ho, to bhi apne ghar ko chhodkar paradesh chale jaana, achhi baat nahin hai. Avval to ve machhuaare aayenge nahin, aayenge, to hum tairkar neeche baith jaayengi, unke jaal mein aayenge hi nahin. Ek do fans bhi gayi, to poochh se jaal faadkar nikal jaayenge. Bhai, shastron aur gyaaniyon ke vachanon ke viruddh, main to nahin jaaungi. Vyavaharikbuddhi ne kaha, main shastron ke baare mein nahin jaanti, magar meri buddhi kehti hai, ki manushya jaise taakatwar aur bhayaanak shatru ki aashanka sir par ho, to bhaagkar kahin chhup jao. Aisa kehte hue, vo apne anuyayiyon ko lekar chal padi.
Kuch bhaari man se, wo Guru ji ke paas gaya, aur saara vrittant keh sunaya. Pratiyogita shuru hui, pehle charan ki shuruaat kauve ne ki, aur ek se badhkar ek kalaabaziyaan dikhane laga. Wo kabhi gol-gol chakkar khata, to kabhi zameen chhoote hue, upar ud jaata. Wahin, hans uske mukable kuch khaas nahi kar paaya. Kauwa ab aur bhi badh-chadh kar bolne laga, main to pehle hi keh raha tha, ki tum logon ko aur kuch bhi nahi aata.
Ek yuva nar hans ne kauwe ki chunauti sveekar kar li. Ye tay hua, ki pratiyogita do charanon mein hogi, pehle charan mein kauwa, apne kartab dikhayega, aur hans ko bhi wahi karke dikhana hoga, aur doosre charan mein, kauwe ko hans ke kartab, dohraane honge.
Hanson ka ek jhund, samudra tat ke upar se guzarr raha tha. Usii jagah, ek kauwa bhi mauj masti kar raha tha. Usne hanson ko, upeksha bhari nazron se dekha. Tum log kitni achhi udaan bhar lete ho. Kauwa mazak ke lahje mein bola, tum log aur kar hi kya sakte ho, bas apna pankh phadphada kar, udaan bhar sakte ho. Kya tum meri tarah phurti se ud sakte ho. Meri tarah, hawa mein kalabaziyaan dikha sakte ho. Nahin, tum to theek se jaante bhi nahin ki udna kise kehte hain.
Par hans ne koi jawab nahi diya, aur chup-chaap udta raha. Dheere-dheere, ve zameen se bahut door hote gaye, aur kauwe ka badbadana bhi, kam hota gaya, aur kuch der mein bilkul hi band ho gaya. Kauwa ab buri tarah thak chuka tha, itna, ki ab uske liye khud ko hava mein rakhna bhi mushkil ho raha tha, aur wo baar-baar, paani ke kareeb pahuch raha tha. Hans, kauwe ki sthiti, samajh raha tha, par usne anjaan bante hue kaha, tum baar-baar paani kyun chhoo rahe ho, kya ye bhi tumhara koi kartab hai. Nahin, kauwa bola, mujhe maaf kar do, main ab bilkul thak chuka hoon, aur yadi tumne meri madad nahi ki, toh main yahin dam tod doonga. Mujhe bacha lo, main kabhi ghamand nahi dikhaoonga.

Use is kadar bhaagta dekhte hue, ek anya gadhe ne usse poocha, are kya hua bhai, tum is tarah behavas bhaage kyun ja rahe ho?
Ye sunkar doosra gadha bhi dar gaya, aur uske saath, bhaagne laga. Ab to wo dono ek saath chilla rahe the, bhago-bhago dharti fat rahi hai.
Sab ek doosre ka muhn dekhne lage, fir bandar bola, mujhe to ye baat cheetey ne batayi thi. Cheetey ne kaha, maine to ye pakshiyon se suna tha. Aur aise karte karte pata chala, ki ye baat, sabse pehle gadhe ne batayi thi.
Late-late uske mann mein bure khayal aane lage. Usne socha, yadi dharti fat gayi, to mera kya hoga. Abhi usne aisa socha hi tha, ki use ek zor se dhamake ki aawaz aayi. Wo bhaybheet ho utha, aur cheekhne laga, bhago-bhago, dharti fat rahi hai, apni jaan bachao. Aur aisa kehte hue, wo pagalon ki tarah ek disha mein bhaagne laga.
Dekhte-dekhte saikdon gadhe is baat ko dohrate hue, usi disha mein bhaagne lage. Gadho ko is tarah bhaagta dekh, anya jaanwar bhi dar gaye. Dharti phatne ki khabar jungle mein lagi aag ki tarah, failne lagi, aur jald hi sabko pata chal gaya, ki dharti phat rahi hai. Chaaron taraf jaanwaro ki cheekh-pukaar mach gayi. Saanp, bichchhu, siyaar, lomad, haathi, ghode, sabhi us jhund mein, shaamil ho, bhaagne lage.

Chidiya use samjhaane lagi, are yahan toh khidki se tez hawa aati hai. Yahan toh tu apne jaale ke saath hi ud jaayegi.
Isiliye, humein kisi gadhe ki baat par yakeen karne se pehle, apna dimaag, zaroor laga lena chahiye, aur ye bhi samajhna chahiye, ki agar saikron log bhi kisi galat cheez ko badhava de rahe hain, to bhi wo galat hi rahti hai, aur usse bachne mein hi, bhalaai hai.
Theek hai, chalo, mujhe us jagah le chalo, aur dikhao, ki dharti phat rahi hai. Aisa kehte hue, sher gadhe ko us taraf dhakelta hua le jaane laga. Baaki jaanwar bhi unke peeche ho liye, aur dar-dar kar, us or, badhne lage. Bargad ke paas pahunch kar gadha bola, huzoor, main yahaan so raha tha, ki tabhi zor se, dharti phatne ki aawaz aayi. Ye baat, makdi ke gale utar gayi. Usne acchi salah ke liye billi ko dhanyavaad diya, aur jaala adhoora chhodkar, doosri jagah talash karne lagi. Usne idhar udhar dekha. Use ek khidki nazar aayi, aur usne jaala bunna shuru kiya. Kuch der tak vo jaala bunti rahi, tabhi ek chidiya aayi, aur makdi ka mazak udate hue boli, Are makdi, tu bhi kitni bevakoof hai.
Ek makdi thi. Usne aaraam se rehne ke liye, ek shandar jaala banane ka vichar kiya, aur socha, ki is jaale mein khoob keedein, makkhiyaan faseengi, aur main use aahaar banuungi, aur maze se rahungi. Usne kamre ke ek kone ko pasand kiya, aur wahan jaala bunna shuru kiya. Kuch der baad, aadha jaala bun kar tayaar ho gaya. Ye dekhkar, wo makdi kaafi khush hui, ki tabhi achanak uski nazar, ek billi par padi, jo use dekhkar, hans rahi thi.
Sher ne aas paas ja kar dekha, aur saara maamla samajh gaya. Usne sabhi ko sambodhit karte hue kaha, ye gadha mahaamoorkh hai. Darasal, paas hi nariyal ka ek uncha ped hai, aur tez hawa chalne se, us par laga ek bada sa nariyal, neeche patthar par gir pada. Patthar sarakne se, aas-paas dhool udne lagi, aur ye gadha na jaane kaise, ise dharti fatne ki baat samajh baitha. Ek baar, ek kisaan ne apne padosi ko bhala bura keh diya. Par jab baad mein use apni galti ka ehsaas hua, to wo ek sant ke paas gaya. Usne sant se, apne shabd wapas lene ka upaay poocha.

Chinti boli, main bahut der se tumhe dekh rahi thi, tum baar-baar apna kaam shuru karti, aur doosron ke kehne par, use adhoora chhod deti. Aur jo log aisa karte hain, unki yahi haalat hoti hai. Aur aisa kehte hue wo apne raste chali gayi, aur makdi pachhtati hui, nidhall padi rahi.

Kakroach bola, are, yahaan kahaan jaala bunne chali aayi. Ye to bekaar ki almirah hai. Abhi ye yahaan padi hai, kuch dinon baad ise bech diya jaayega, aur tumhari saari mehnat bekaar chale jaayegi. Ye sun kar, makri ne wahan se hatt jaana hi behtar samjha.
Makdi ko chidiya ki baat theek lagi, aur wo wahan bhi jaala adhoora bana chhodkar sochne lagi, ab kahan jaala banaya jaye. Samay kaafi beet chuka tha, aur ab use bhookh bhi lagne lagi thi. Ab use ek almarai ka khula darwaza dikha, aur usne usi mein, apna jaala bunna shuru kiya. Kuch jaala buna hi tha, tabhi use ek cockroach nazar aaya, jo jaale ko achraaj bhare nazron se dekh raha tha.
Ek mantri ne Vishnusharma ka naam bataya. Mantri ne kaha, Maharaj, Vishnusharma ek bahut hi gyani purush hain, jo apne sau se adhik shishyoon ke saath rahte hain. Wo hi aapke putron ko sahi shiksha de paayenge. Aap unki sharan mein jaayen, aur aapko bahut jald hi badlaav dikhega.
Ek samay ki baat hai. Ek talaab ke kinaare, ek kachhua, aur do hans rahte the. Kachhua, talaab mein rahata tha. Uski hanson ke saath dosti ho gayi thi, jo usse milne, hamesha talaab tak aate rahte the. Sab bahut khushi khushi miljul kar rahte the.
Sokrat ne pucha, jab tum wahan the, to tum sabse zyada kya chahte the. Ladke ne uttar diya, saans lena. Sokrat ne kaha, yahi safalta ka rahasya hai. Jab tum safalta ko utni hi buri tarah se chahoge, jitna ki tum saans lena chahte the, to wo tumhe mil jaayegi. Iske alawa aur koi rahasya nahi hai.
Ek saal, wahan akal pada. Bahut dinon tak baarish nahi hui. Sab khet khalihan, talab sookh gaye. Paani ki ek boond bhi nahi bachi, kisi ke peene ke liye. Saare jaanwar, paani ke aabhav, aur tez garmi ki wajah se, marne lage. Tab bahut saare jaanwaron ne, doosri jagah jaana tay kiya, jahan par paani bhi ho, aur khet-khalihan, hare-bhare hon.
Shahar ke logon ne aisa nazara pehli baar dekha tha. Sabhi bahut aashcharyachakit hue. Sabhi log hansne lage, aur taaliyan bajane lage, hanso aur kachhue ko aise udte dekh kar. Log zor zor se halla karne lage, aur hansne lage. Ye sab dekh kar kachhue ko gussa aane laga. Apni jigyasa ko rokne ki bajay, usne bolne ke liye munh khola, aur uski pakad, chhoot gayi, aur wo gir kar mar gaya. Is tarah, kachhua, apni murkhta, aur besabri se, maara gaya.
Ek samay ki baat hai. Amarasakti naam ka ek raja, Dakshin Bharat mein raaj karta tha. Uske teen kaamchor putra the, jo uski chinta ke kaaran ban chuke the. Jab raja ko yeh gyaan hua, ki uske putron ko kaam seekhne mein koi ruchi nahi hai, to raja ne apne mantriyon ko bula kar kaha, aap logon ko to pata hi hai, ki main apne putron se khush nahi hoon. Gyaani purushon ne kaha hai, ki ajanm putra, murkh putra se behtar hote hain. Murkh putra, apne pita ke liye apmaan ka kaaran banta hai. Main unhe, apna uttaradhikari banne ke yogya kaise banaun. Mera maargdarshan karein.

Teenon dost, kachhua, aur hanson ne bhi, us talaab ko chhodkar, kahin aur jaane ka faisla kiya, jahaan bahut paani ho, aur wahin hamesha ke liye basne ka vichar kiya. Par doosri jagah jaana bhi mushkil tha. Hanson ke liye to aasan tha, kyunki, unhe udna aata tha. Par kachhua ke liye ye bahut hi mushkil kaam tha. Teenon doston ne paramarsh karke is pareshani ka hal nikalne ki sochi. Ek baar ek naujawan ladke ne Sukraat se poocha, ki safalta ka rahasya kya hai. Sukraat ne us ladke se kaha, ki tum kal mujhe nadi ke kinare milo. Wo mile. Ladka baahar nikalne ke liye sangharsh karne laga, lekin Sukraat taakatwar the, aur use tab tak duboye rakhe, jab tak ki wo neela nahi padne laga. Ek baar ki baat hai. Ek ped ki choti par ek ghosla tha, jismein ek kauwe ki jodi rahti thi. Lekin durbhagya se, us ped ke tal par, ek naag bhi rahta tha. Kawe ne apne mitr siyar se sampark kiya, aur usko saari baat batayi. Siyar kawe se bola, ki tum raja ke mahal jao, aur wahan se ek mehngi vastu lao, aur use naag ke bil mein phenk do. Vyapari ki baat sunte hi Guru ji saari baat samajh gaye, aur bole, hairani aur pareshani chhodo. Darasal, jo gaav wale pujari hain, unka achha swabhav hi hai, jo log usi devalay mein jaana chahte hain, jahan ve hote hain. Unka logon se nishwarth prem, unke dukh se dukhi hona, unke sukh mein prasann hona, unse mitrata ka vyavhaar karna hi, logon ko unki aur aakarshit karta hai, aur log svatah hi, unki aur khinche chale aate hain. Ab saari baat vyapari ki samajh mein aa chuki thi.
Vyavaharik buddhi se humara aashay hai, ki kis samay mein humein kya karna chahiye, aur jo hum kar rahe hain, us karya ka parinaam nikalne par, kya samasyaayein aa sakti hain, yeh sochna hi, vyavaharik buddhi hai. Bolchaal ki bhasha mein, hum ise common sense bhi kahte hain, aur bhale hi hum bade gyaani na hon, moti moti kitaabein na padhi hon, lekin hum apni vyavaharik buddhi se, kisi paristhiti ka saamna aasani se kar sakte hain.
Kuch bhaari man se vah guru ji ke paas gaya, aur saara vrittant kah sunaaya. Guru ji ne kuch vichar kiya, aur phir use yah paramaresh diya, ki vah gaon ke mandir ke pujari ko, nagar ke mandir mein seva ke liye bula le. Usne aisa hi kiya, nagar ke pujari ko gaon, aur gaon ke pujari ko nagar mein seva par niyukt kar diya. Kuch hi din beete the, ki vah yah dekhkar stabdh rah gaya, ki ab gaon ke log nagar ke mandir ki aur rukh karne lage hain. Ab to use hairaani ke saath saath pareshani bhi anubhav hone lagi. Bina ek kshan ki der ke, vah guruji ke paas ja kar haath jod kar kehne laga, aapki aagyaanusaar maine dono pujariyon ka sthaanantar kiya, lekin samasya to pehle se bhi gambheer ho chali hai, ki ab to mere gaon ke parichit aur parijan, kasht sahkar aur kiraya bhaada kharch karke, nagar ke devalay mein aane lage hain. Mujhse yah nahin dekha jaata.
Mitron, humein bhi yeh baat achche se samajhni chahiye, ki hamara vyaktitva, humare baahari rang roop se nahi, hamare vyavhaar se nirdhaarit hota hai, bilkul ek samaan gyaan aur vesh bhusha wale do pujariyon mein, log kasht sehkar bhi usi ke paas gaye, jo adhik sanvedansheel aur vyavhaari tha. Gadha bahut lajjit hua, geedar ki chaal bhari baatein hi aisi thi. Gadha fir uske saath chal pada. Jungle mein jhaadi ke paas pahunchte hi, sher ne nukile panjhon se use maar giraaya. Is prakar, sher aur geedar ka bhojan joota.
Chacha, tumhein shaayad pata nahi, ki jungle mein ek bagula Bhagatji ka satsang hua tha. Uske baad, saare jaanwar shaakahari ban gaye hain. Ab koi kisi ko nahi khata. Geedar bola, aur kaan ke paas mooh le jaakar daana phenka, Chachu, paas ke kasbe se bechaari gadhi bhi apne dhobi maalik ke atyacharon se tang aakar, jungle mein aa gayi thi. Wahan hari hari ghaas khaakar, vah khoob lehra gayi hain, tum uske saath ghar basa lena.
Gadhe ke dimaag par hari hari ghaas aur ghar basane ke sunahare sapne chhaane lage. Wah gidaad ke saath, jungle ki or chal diya. Jungle mein gidaad, gadhe ko usi jhaadi ke paas le gaya, jismein sher chhipa baitha tha. Isse pehle ki sher panja maarta, gadhe ko jhaadi mein sher ki neeli battiyaan ki tarah chamakti aankhein nazar a gayi. Wah darkar uchhla, gadha bhaaga, aur bhaagta hi gaya. Sher bujhe svar mein gidaad se bola, bhai is baar main tayaar nahi tha. Tum use dobara lao, is baar galti nahi hogi.
Ek din kauwe ne socha, waise to ye chalaak khargosh mere haath aayenge nahi, agar inka narm maans khana hai, to mujhe bhi baaz ki tarah karna hoga. Ekaek jhapta maar kar pakad loonga.
Ek baar ki baat hai, ek khargosh, bahut dhinge maar raha tha, ki wo kitna teevr bhaag sakta hai, aur wo jungle mein rehne wale kachhue ka upahaas kar raha tha, ki wo kitna dheema hai. Yah sun kar, kachhue ne khargosh ko daud ki chunauti de di. Dono ne daud karne ka nirnay liya.
Kanchanpur ke ek dhani vyaapaari ke ghar mein, rasoi mein ek kabootar ne ghosla bana rakha tha. Kisi din ek laalchi kauwa udhar se aa nikla. Wahan machhli ko dekhkar, uske muh mein paani aa gaya. Tab uske mann mein vichar aaya, ki mujhe is rasoi ghar mein ghusna chahiye, lekin kaise ghusoo, ye sochkar wo pareshaan tha. Tabhi uski nazar, wo kabootaron ke ghosle par padi.
Dusre din kauwe ne bhi ek khargosh ko dabochne ki baat sochkar, oonchi udaan bhari. Phir usne khargosh ko pakadne ke liye, baaz ki tarah zor se jhatta maara. Ab bhala kauaa baaz ka kya mukabla karta. Khargosh ne use dekh liya, aur jhat, wahan se bhaagkar chattan ke peeche chhip gaya. Kauaa apni hi jhonk mein us chattan se ja takraaya. Nateeja, uski choanch aur gardan toot gayi, aur usne wahiin tadap kar dam tod diya. Isliye kehte hain, nakal karne ke liye bhi akal chahiye.
Ek samay ki baat thi, ek pahaad ki unchi choti par, ek baaz rehta tha. Pahaad ki tarai mein, bargad ke ped par ek kauwa apna ghosla banakar rehta tha. Woh bada chalak aur dhurt tha. Uska prayaas sada yahi rehta tha, ki bina mehnat kiye khane ko mil jaaye. Ped ke aaspaas, khoh mein khargosh rehte the. Jab bhi khargosh bahar aate, to baaz unchi udaan bharte, aur ekadh khargosh ko uthaakar le jaate.
Ek baar ki baat hai, ek ped ki choti par ek ghosla tha, jis mein ek kauwe ki ek jodi rahti thi. Lekin durbhagya se us ped ke tal par, ek naag bhi rehta tha. Jab bhi maada kauwa koi anda deti, aur jaise hi kauwe ki jodi ped se door jaati, tabhi, wo naag rengta hua ped ke upar jaata, aur ghosle mein rakha kauwe ka anda kha jaata. Jab kauwe ki jodi wapas aaye, to yeh dekh bahut dukhi hue, aur jab ye baar baar hua, tab kauwe ki jodi ne, us naag se chhutkara paane ka nirnay kar liya.
Jaisa ki sabne socha tha, khargosh, daud praarambh hote hi teevrata se kachhua se aage nikal gaya. Abhi daudte daudte thoda hi samay guzra tha, ki khargosh ne peeche mudkar dekha, ki kachhua kaafi peeche reh gaya hai. Usne socha, ki kachhua ki chaal to bahut hi dheemi hai, isliye main thodi der vishraam kar leta hoon. Woh ek ped ki thandi chhaav mein aisa soya, ki kachhua, dheemi chaal hone ke bawajood bhi, usse aage nikal kar apne gantevya tak pahunch kar daud jeet gaya. Jab khargosh ne neend se utha, to use kachhua dikhai nahi diya. Khargosh daud jeetne ke liye gantevya ki aur dauda, aur aashchary mein, kachhua ko wahan uski prateeksha karta paaya.
Kauwe ne apne mitr siyaar se sampark kiya, aur usko saari baat batai. Siyaar kauwe se bola, ki tum raja ke mahal jao, aur wahan se, ek mahangi vastu laane, aur use naag ke bil mein phenkne ke liye kaha. Kauaa raja ke mahal gaya, aur usne rani ke kamre se uska haar chura liya. Rani ne yeh dekh liya, aur mahal ki rakshak ko, kauwe se wo haar wapas lene ke liye kaha. Rakshak, kauwe ke peeche peeche, jungle ki ore gaya. Kauaa jab ped ke paas pahunchaa, tab usne rani ka haar, naag ke bil mein phenk diya. Rakshak ne yeh dekh liya, aur us bil se haar wapas lene ke liye, rakshak ne, bil mein rehne wale naag ko maar diya, aur bil se haar wapas le liya. Is tarah se kauwe ki jodi, naag se chutkaara paane mein safal rahi.
Usne socha, ki agar main kabooter se dosti kar loon, to shayad meri baat ban jaayein. Kabooter jab daana chugne ke liye baahar nikalta hai, to kauwa uske saath nikalta hai. Thodi der baad kabooter peeche mudkar dekhta hai, to dekha, ki kauwa uske peeche hai. Is par kabooter ne kauwe se kaha, bhai tum mere peeche kyun ho. Is par kauwe ne kabooter se kaha, ki tum mujhe achhe lagte ho, isliye main tumse dosti karna chahta hoon. Is par kauwe se kabooter ne kaha, ki hum kaise dost ban sakte hain. Hamara aur tumhara bhojan bhi to alag alag hai. Main beej khata hoon, aur tum keede. Is par kauwe ne chaaploosi dikhate hue kaha, kaunsi badi baat hai, mere paas ghar nahi hai, isliye hum saath saath to reh hi sakte hain, aur saath hi bhojan khojne aaya karenge, tum apna, aur main apna.
Ek samay ki baat thi, ek raja ne, ek paltoo bandar ko apne sevak ke roop mein rakha hua tha. Jahan jahan raja jaata, vah bandar bhi uske saath jaata. Raja ke darbaar mein, us bandar ko raja ka paltoo hone ke kaaran, koi rok tok nahi thi. Ek garmi ke mausam ke ek din, raja apne shayan par vishraam kar raha tha. Vah bandar bhi, shayan ke paas baith kar, raja ko ek pankhe se hawa kar raha tha. Tabhi ek makhhi aayi, aur raja ki chhati par aakar baith gayi. Jab bandar ne us makhhi ko baitha dekha, to usne use udaane ka prayaas kiya. Har baar, vo makhhi udti, aur thodi der baad, fir raja ki chhati par aakar baith jaati. Yah dekh kar, bandar gusse se laal ho gaya. Gusse mein usne makhhi ko maarne ki thaani. Fir vo bandar, makhhi ko maarne ke liye hathiyaar dhoondhne laga. Kuch door hi, use raja ki talwaar dikhai di. Usne vo talwaar uthayi, aur gusse mein, makhhi ko maarne ke liye poore bal se talwaar raja ki chhati par maar di. Isse pehle ki talwaar makhhi ko lagti, makhhi vahaan se ud gayi. Bandar ke bal se kiye gaye vaar se, makhhi to nahi mari, magar usse raja ki mrityu avashya ho gayi. Isliye kehte hain, ki moorkh ko apna sevak banane mein koi bhalai nahi!
Ek tota tha, Meethuram. Pinjra hi Meethuram ka ghar tha, aur wahi uski duniya. Meethuram ki awaaz badi achi thi, par wah sirf raat ko hi gata tha.
Meethuram ne iski wajah batate hue kaha, ki ek baar jab main jungle mein din ke samay gaana gaa raha tha, to ek shikaari udhar se nikla. Usne meri awaaz suni, aur usi kaaran, usne mujhe pakad liya. Tabse abhi tak main is pinjre mein kaid hoon.
Wah udkar talaab ke kinare gaya, aur shahad si meethi boli mein kehne laga, mitra, tum to bahut chust durust ho. Ek hi jhatke mein machhli ko apni chonch mein fasa lete ho, mujhe bhi ye kala sikha do.
Unmein se ek kauwa kauvi ne, ped par apna basera kar liya. Us ped ke neeche ek talab tha, jismein jalkauwa rehta tha. Wah saare din paani mein khade rahkar, kabhi machhliyaan pakadta, kabhi paani ki satah par pankh phailakar, lehron ke saath naachta nazar aata.

Ek desh mein akal pada. Paani ki kami se, saari fasle maari gayin. Deshvasi, apne liye ek vakt ki roti bhi nahi jhuta paate the. Aise samay kauvon ko roti ke tukde milne band ho gaye. Ve jungle ki or ud chale.
Sach bhi hai, ki kai baar hum galtiyan karne ke baad hi usse kuch na kuch seekhte hain. Par zaroori nahi hai, ki har baar seekhne ke liye galti hi ki jaye. Kai martaba, kisi kaam ko karne se pehle, kuch saavdhaniyan barat kar hum galtiyon se bach sakte hain, aur nuksan se bhi. Toh yaad rakhiye, buddhimaan wahi hota hai, jo soch vichar kar kaam karta hai.

Are dost! Yeh kya kar rahe ho? Tum paani mein mat jao. Tum thal kauwa ho, jal kauwa nahi. Tum jal mein machhli pakadne ke daanpench nahi jaante, musibat mein pad jaoge.

Apni raksha ka upay sochne ke liye, khargoshon ne ek sabha bulayi. Sabha mein bahut se khargosh ikatthe hue. Khargoshon ke sardaar ne haathiyon ke atyacharon ka varnan karte hue kaha, kya hammein se koi aisa hai, jo apni jaan par khelkar haathiyon ka atyachar band kara sake?

Haathi jab khargoshon ki basti se nikalne lagte, to chhote chhote khargosh, unke pairon ke neeche aa jaate the. Kuch khargosh mar jaate the, kuch ghaayal ho jaate the.

Haathi wahan bhojan aur paani paakar bade prasann hue.

Khargosh Gajaraj ko chandrama ke paas le jaane ke liye tayaar ho gaya. Usne kaha, main tumhe chandrama ke paas le chal sakta hoon, par shart ye hai, ki tum, akele hi chaloge. Gajaraj ne khargosh ki baat maan li.

Mantharak tatkal jal se nikla. Dono ek dusre se milkar prasannachit the. Isi beech, Hiranyak bhi aa pahunchaa. Laghuponak ne Mantharak se Hiranyak ka parichay karaya, tatha uske gunon ki prashansa bhi ki.
Mantharak ne bhi, Hiranyak se uske janmsthaan se vairagya ka kaaran jaana chaha. Dono ke aagrah ko sunkar, Hiranyak apni vyatha katha sunaane laga.
Maine dhan ko punah praapt karne ki kai koshish ki, lekin kadi nigraani ke kaaran, mujhe wo wapas nahin mil paaya. Is kaaran mere parijan bhi, mujhse kanni kaatne lage the. Is prakaar, main daridrata, tatha apmaan ki zindagi jee raha tha.
Dono mitron ne saath jaane ka nishchay kiya. Hiranyak, Laghupatnak ke peeth par baithkar, us sarovar ki aur prasthaan kar gaya. Nishchit sthan par pahunchkar, kauwe ne chooha ko apni peeth se utaara, tatha talab ke kinare khade hokar, apne mitr, Mantharak ko pukarne laga.
Pareshan hokar sanyasi ek phate baans ka danda lekar aaya. Dande ki aawaaz se, hum log dar jaate the, lekin uske so jaate hi, punah handiyaa saaf kar dete the.
Hiranyak ne bataya, ki apni saathi ki baat sunkar, ek raat main wahan aaya, tatha khunti par latki haandi par chhalaang laga diya, tatha haandi ko neeche gira diya, tatha saathiyon ke saath, swaadisht bhojan ka aanand liya. Ab yeh hamara, har raat ka niyam sa ban gaya.
Vrihat sphik ne, jigyasa dikhate hue poocha, chooha ka bil kahan hai? Taamrachood ne, anabhigyata darshayi, lekin yeh spasht tha, ki zaroor hi yeh bil kisi khazane par hai. Dhan ki garmi ke kaaran hi, yeh chooha, utna adhik unchai tak kood sakta hai. Vrihatasphik ne, ek kudaal mangwaya, tatha nishchit hokar raat mein dono so gaye.

Dheere dheere Hiranyak bhi, apne dhan ki kshati ko bhool gaya, tatha sukhpoorvak jeevan yaapan karne laga.
Khatmal bola, lekin main tumhara mehmaan hoon, mujhe kuch to dogi khane ke liye. Aur raja ke khoon se badhiya bhojan aur kya ho sakta hai.
Joon antatah khatmal ki chikni chupdi baaton mein aa gayi, aur use sharan dete hue boli, theek hai, tum yahan raatbhar ruk sakte ho, lekin raja ko kaatoge to nahi, uska khoon choosne ke liye.

Ek baar ki baat hai, ek jungle mein ek sher tha. Wah sher, bahut gamandi aur gusse wala tha. Wah apni bhukh ke liye hi nahi, apitu, apne manoranjan ke liye jantuon ki hatya kiya karta tha. Sare jantuon ne, sher ke is prakop se pareshan hokar, yah nirnay liya, ki unhe is vishay par sher se baat karni chahiye. Unhone ek baar sher ko nimantran par bulaya. Wahan sare jantu bhi ekatrit hue. Wahan haathi, khargosh, hiran, bhaalu, bandar, lomdi, chooha, gaay, bais, gilihari, baarasingha aadi the. Unhone sher se kaha, ki agar sher, isi tarah se jungle mein jantuon ka shikar karta raha, to wah din door nahi, jab sare jantu, jungle se lupt ho jayenge. Unhone sher ke saamne ek prasthav rakha. Prasthav ke anusaar, ek ek kar, har ek din ek jantu sher ke bhojan ke liye uski guffa mein bhej diya jayega. Ek tarah sher apne bhojan ke alawa, jantuon ka shikar nahi kar payega. Is prasthav se, jantuon ko bhi chain milega. Sher ne yah prasthav, sveekar kar liya. Sher ke liye, ye sahi bhi tha, kyunki ab use shikar karne ke liye apni guffa se baahar bhi nahi jaana padega. Us din ke baad se, har din ek jantu, sher ke liye bheja jane laga.
Ek baar ek khargosh ki baari aayi. Wah khargosh bahut chatur tha, aur use ek upaay soojha. Wah khargosh, sher ke paas kuch der se gaya. Is par sher bahut gussa hua, aur jab usne ek chhote se khargosh ko dekha, to usse aur bhi gussa aaya. Sher gusse mein bola, ki main saare jantuon ko kha jaunga. Khargosh bola, ki ismein uska koi dosh nahin hai. Uske bhojan ke liye paanch khargosh bheje gaye the, magar raste mein chaar khargoshon ko, ek doosra sher kha gaya, aur wah, ek lota khargosh apni jaan bachakar uske paas aaya. Is par sher bola, us jungle mein keval wahi sher hai, aur khargosh, use us jagah par lekar jaaye, jahan usne doosra sher dekha tha. Khargosh, us sher ko ek kuen ke paas lekar chala gaya, aur bola, ki usne doosre sher ko us kuen ke andar dekha tha. Sher ne jab us kuen mein dekha, to use apni chhavi dikhai di. Apni chhavi dekh kar, sher ko laga ki us kuen mein doosra sher hai. Sher ne usse ladaai kar, use apne jungle se bahar karne ki sochi, aur yeh soch kar, us kuen mein chhalang laga di. Aisa kar, sher ne apni jaan gawa di. Is tarah khargosh ne na keval apni, parantu doosre jantuon ki bhi jaan bacha li.

Yah sunkar chatur khatmal to palang ke paaye ke neeche chhip gaya, lekin chadar ke kone par baithi joon, raja ke sevakon ki nazar mein aa gayi. Unhone use pakda, aur maar daala.
Kisaano ne ladke ki awaaz suni, to ve apna apna kaam chhodkar, ladke ki madad ke liye daud pade. Jo bhi haath laga, saath le aaye. Koi faawda le aaya, koi daraanti, to koi hansiya. Magar jab ve ladke ke paas pahunche, to unhein kahin bhediya dikhai nahi diya.

Ve pehle ki tarah apne kaam kaaj mein judi rahi. Naag ne yah dekha, to uske krodh ka paaravaar na raha. Wah gusse mein bharkar baambi ke nikat ja pahucha. Yah dekh, hazaaron chintiyan, us baambi se nikal padi, aur naag se lipatkar, uske sharir par kaatne lagi. Unke kantile dankon se pareshan naag bilbilane laga. Uski peeda asahniya ho chuki thi, aur sharir par ghaav hone lage the. Naag ne chintiyon ko hataane ki bahut koshish ki, lekin asafal raha. Kuch hi der mein, usne wahi tadap tadap kar jaan de di.
Aakhirkar usne bill ko chhodkar, ek vishal ped ke neeche rehne ki sochi. Lekin wahin ped ki jad mein, chintiyon ki baambi thi, aur unke saath rehna, naag ke liye asambhav tha. So, wah naag un chintiyon ki baambi ke nikat jaakar bola, main sarpraj naag hoon, is jungle ka raja. Main tum chintiyon ko aadesh deta hoon, ki yeh jagah chhodkar chale jaao.
